***жертва.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жертва.html>же́ртва</a> (1382)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*žьrtva</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sacrifice</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*žьrti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sacrifice</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-tva</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*girʔ-</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*GʷrH-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жертва.html>же́ртва</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žértva</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жертва.html>же́ртвы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жертва.html>же́ртвы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жертва.html>же́ртв</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sacrifice
<dl><dd><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white">Иакинф (Бичурин), <i><a href = vnd.unilang:собрание.html>Собра́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сведение.html>сведений</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:народ.html>наро́дах</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:обитавший.html>обита́вших</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>Сре́дней</a> Азии <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:древний.html>дре́вние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>времена́</a></i> 1851:<dl><dd><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обыкновенный.html>обыкнове́нно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пятый.html>пятой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:луна.html>луне́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́нии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:полевой.html>полевы́х</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́т</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:приносить.html>прино́сят</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:жертва.html>же́ртву</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дух.html>ду́хам</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Obyknovénno v pjatoj luné, po okončánii polevýx rabót, prinósjat <b>žértvu</b> duxam.</i></dd><dd>The fifth moon, after the fieldwork is done, they usually offer a <b>sacrifice</b> to the spirits.</dd></dl></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>victim</li>
<li>casualty</li></ol>

***жертвовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жертвовать.html>же́ртвовать</a> (11907)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жертва.html>же́ртва</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žértva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жертвовать.html>же́ртвовать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žértvovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пожертвовать.html>поже́ртвовать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to donate</li>
<li>to sacrifice, to give, to offer
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:жертвовать.html>же́ртвовать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>собо́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>žértvovatʹ</b> sobój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sacrifice oneself</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:жертвовать.html>же́ртвовать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жи́знью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>žértvovatʹ</b> žíznʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sacrifice [lay down] one's life</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:увеличить.html>увели́чить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:производство.html>произво́дство</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:жертвовать.html>же́ртвуя</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:качество.html>ка́чеством</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">uvelíčitʹ proizvódstvo, ne <b>žértvuja</b> káčestvom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">increase production without sacrificing quality</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:жертвовать.html>же́ртвовать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:конь.html>коня́</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">chess</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>žértvovatʹ</b> konjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sacrifice a knight</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***жертвуемый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жертвовать.html>же́ртвуемый</a> (11907)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жесткость.html>жёсткость</a> (14477)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жесткий.html>жёсткий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žóstkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жесткость.html>жёсткость</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žóstkostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жесткость.html>жёсткости</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жесткость.html>жёсткости</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жесткость.html>жёсткостей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>rigidity, inflexibility</li>
<li>hardness</li>
<li>inclemency</li>
<li>acerbity</li>
<li>harshness, asperity</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жестокий.html>жесто́кий</a> (2546)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">жестокъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žestokŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">жестъкъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žestŭkŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жесткий.html>жёсткий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žóstkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жестокий.html>жесто́кий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žestókij</span>) (<i>rare/awkward comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)жесто́че</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cruel</li>
<li>brutal, savage</li></ol>

***жесть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жесть.html>жесть</a> (12111)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mongolic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Mongolic languages">Mongolic</a></span> borrowing. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kazakh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Kazakh language">Kazakh</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="kk">жез</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="kk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jez</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">brass</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tatar language">Tatar</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="tt">җиз</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="tt-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ciz</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">brass</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mongolian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Mongolian language">Mongolian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="mn">зэс</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="mn-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zes</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">copper, brass</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Remodeled under the influence of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жесть.html>жесть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žestʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">frozen soil</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жесть.html>жесть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žestʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жесть.html>же́сти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жесть.html>же́сти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жесть.html>же́стей</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жестяной.html>жестяно́й</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жетон.html>жето́н</a> (15554)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">jeton</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***жечь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жечь.html>жечь</a> (5386)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">жечи</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žeči</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*žeťi</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to burn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> lt; <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gegti</i> lt; <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*degti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*degtéi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰégʷʰeti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жечь.html>жечь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žečʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пожечь.html>поже́чь</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сжечь.html>сжечь</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поджечь.html>подже́чь</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разжечь.html>разже́чь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to burn</li>
<li>to torment</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:живой.html>живо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">živój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***живой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:живой.html>живо́й</a> (3524)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*živъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʷih₃wós</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">alive</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">quick</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">vīvus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:живой.html>живо́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">živój</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)живе́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)живе́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>living, live, alive
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:живой.html>живо́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:звук.html>звук</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>živój</b> zvuk</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>live</b> sound (for television programs)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>lively, vivid, vivacious, animated</li>
<li>quick, nimble, brisk</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наглядный.html>нагля́дный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nagljádnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реальный.html>реа́льный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">reálʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***живот.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:живот.html>живо́т</a> (1058)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*životъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:живот.html>живо́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">živót</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:живот.html>живота́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:живот.html>животы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:живот.html>живото́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>belly, stomach</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> life</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:живот.html>живо́т</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">živót</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***живучий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:живучий.html>живу́чий</a> (15761)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">жив-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">živ-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-у́чий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-účij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:живучий.html>живу́чий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">živúčij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>viable, of great vitality, tenacious <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in life</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:живучий.html>живу́чий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кошка.html>ко́шка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">živúčij kak kóška</i> ― <span class="e-translation">having nine lives like a cat; as tenacious as a cat</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>enduring, lasting
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:живучий.html>живу́чий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:обычай.html>обы́чай</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>živúčij</b> obýčaj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">durable custom</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
